 i learned some tutorials and learned a bunch 
 although i dont remember the functions exactly i do have an understanding 
 ok 
 gotta start somewhere 
       some of the useful parameters are       
 gameobject   the current gameobject your script is attached to 
 transform   the transform of the gameobject 
       some of the useful methods are       
 gameobject getcomponent componenttype       gets a component of componenttype off the game object  returns null if the component don t exist 
 gameobject find   name      finds a game object in the game with a name 
 instantiate gameobject    makes a clone of the provided gameobject 
 instantiate gameobject  transform  quaternion    makes  a clone of the provided gameobject with a different transform 
 gameobject addcomponent componenttype      adds a component to a gameobject with a specified type  returns the newly added component
